# Comments for Question 2, LLM=Mistral Large 2

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=4.8)
    The plot structure follows a basic problem-solution arc but feels rushed and oversimplified. The metaphorical "monster" and its threat lack sufficient development, while the resolution comes too easily. The cause-effect relationships are present but lack nuance, with Edmund's solution appearing without significant obstacles or complications. The story achieves basic coherence but lacks the tension and complexity needed for a compelling narrative.

  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=6.1)
    The plot has a clear arc—discovery, challenge, transformation—but relies too heavily on abstract concepts rather than concrete events. The connection between unraveling physical knots and overcoming internal fears is thematically sound but mechanically underdeveloped. The garage sales timeframe is mentioned only once without meaningful integration. The resolution feels rushed and overly symbolic rather than earned through specific actions.

  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=4.8)
    The plot lacks clear causality—the discovery of recipes somehow leads to profound personal revelation without sufficient connective tissue. The story tells us about Elias's transformation rather than showing the process. The ending feels rushed and unearned, with forgiveness appearing as a convenient resolution rather than the result of genuine struggle.

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=5.8)

The story achieves coherence but lacks sufficient tension or stakes to drive reader investment.
